        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<p><b>Charlotte Brûlée</b> is the eighth daughter and 19th child of the <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">Charlotte Family</a> and the older twin sister of <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Broy%C3%A9" title="Charlotte Broyé">Broyé</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-mag5_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mag5-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> She is also an <a href="/wiki/Officer" title="Officer">officer</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c930_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c930-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>She was stationed in the Seducing Woods to ambush the Sanji Retrieval Team,<sup id="cite_ref-intro_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> but after being defeated, the team used <a href="/wiki/Mira_Mira_no_Mi" title="Mira Mira no Mi">her Devil Fruit ability</a> to enter an alternate dimension known as <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a> to move around <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c850_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c850-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Due to her actions and role, she is a major antagonist in the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island_Arc" title="Whole Cake Island Arc">Whole Cake Island Arc</a>. She, alongside her siblings <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Katakuri" title="Charlotte Katakuri">Charlotte Katakuri</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Charlotte Oven</a>, become temporary and reluctant allies of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> during <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Film:_Red" title="One Piece Film: Red">One Piece Film: Red</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Brûlée looks in many respects like the stereotypical witch. She is an extremely tall, slightly hunched, and gray-skinned woman with a well-endowed yet thin figure, which makes her limbs appear to be exceptionally long. She stands at roughly twice <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>'s height (170&#160;cm), with her legs alone being noticeably longer than said woman is overall. She also has very long, gnarled fingers with overlong, sharp nails painted blue. The woman's face has very striking, hag-like features. Her droopy eyes have yellow irises and long lashes, and are topped by viridian eye shadow and black, high-arched eyebrows, which she keeps perpetually furrowed. She has a huge and over-projected, reddish hook nose (similar to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">her mother</a>'s), a large mouth with purple lipstick that is usually seen devilishly smiling, a square jaw, and a brown, sharp-cornered scar stretching diagonally down her face from right to left. Brûlée's hair is lavender and divided into two side locks that cascade over her breasts, as well as four other, similarly long, and sharp, lock-like segments that stick to the sides, slightly curved upward.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>She takes to wearing a whitish, creased gown. Its main upper section has a frilly scoop neckline, loose, flaring sleeves that are tattered at the edges, and stops quite below the waist in a frilled hemline, adorned by a horizontal row of red roses above. The lower, seemingly separate part of the dress, which begins under the upper one, falls to the ground and, too, has roses stitched onto itself in the aforementioned manner. Brûlée's clothing is completed by a feathered, sleeveless overcoat in moss green color (the latter, in addition to her grayish skin, earning her comparison to a tree by <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a><sup id="cite_ref-intro_2-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> and to a branch by <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-c836p9_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c836p9-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When she was taken to <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a>'s hideout, her attire is forcefully changed into a more clean and elegant dress by the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Tank_Pirates" title="Fire Tank Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</a>, which is also light in color, with two frilled hemlines and closer-fitting sleeves, as well as a light-colored coat above with actual sleeves and a light fur trim. Her hair was brushed into two sideward wicks.<sup id="cite_ref-c858_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c858-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> But after being saved by Katakuri, she changed her hair back to having four locks.
</p><p>As a young child, Brûlée's hair was shorter and partitioned into eight locks, and her nose was small, cone-shaped, and a paler shade of red. Her skin was also a pale beige-gray color. She wore a white short sleeve dress with flowers around the neckline.<sup id="cite_ref-scar_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-scar-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 162px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 162px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest?cb=20180904204232" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée Anime Concept Art" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/66?cb=20180904204232" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="66" height="150" data-image-name="Brûlée Anime Concept Art.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Anime_Concept_Art.png" data-relevant="1" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Brûlée's concept art from the anime.

</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Brûlée is prideful, as she was rather offended when <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a> referred to her as a talking tree<sup id="cite_ref-intro_2-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> and Luffy called her a branch,<sup id="cite_ref-c836p9_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c836p9-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> as well as when her mother sent <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Cracker" title="Charlotte Cracker">Charlotte Cracker</a> to fight the Straw Hats in her stead due to not considering her powerful enough. Brûlée is confident in her powers and claims that she could kill the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hats</a> in an instant, not liking to be underestimated.<sup id="cite_ref-c836p7_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c836p7-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Due to the terrible scar on her face, she is envious of those with alluring faces to the point that she wants to slice them up.<sup id="cite_ref-c832_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c832-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Her jealousy is also tempered with a very sadistic nature as shown when she intended to boil Carrot alive, Brûlée was excited in disfiguring Carrot's face with horrible burns. She scoffs at the notion of anyone succeeding against an Emperor like Big Mom, believing it to be ridiculous and impossible. She also thinks very little of the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a>, believing their actions in the first half of the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> were not that big of an achievement.<sup id="cite_ref-c837p8-9_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c837p8-9-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Like most of her siblings, Brûlée is arrogant and has the upmost pride in her crew and family. This is shown when she boasted to Luffy about Katakuri's strength and how he had never lost before. This leads her to underestimate her opponents, as she was shocked to learn that Brook managed to get copies of the Poneglyphs and hid them from Big Mom, and became devastated when Katakuri was defeated by Luffy.
</p><p>Brûlée seems to share her mother's dream of creating a paradise with every race united, and finds great joy in discovering new kinds of creatures, especially animals.<sup id="cite_ref-c835p13_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c835p13-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> However, she seems to be extremely close-minded about non-humans, as she considers <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">minks</a> to be mere animals and has no qualms about threatening to consume them, even disregarding their begging for mercy.<sup id="cite_ref-c847_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c847-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> She also thinks very little of her mother's husbands, as she jeeringly declared her ex-stepfather, <a href="/wiki/Pound" title="Pound">Pound</a>, an enemy with no chance of returning from his actions.<sup id="cite_ref-c837p11_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c837p11-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> She also cackled with glee when revealing that none of Big Mom's affiliates could leave her alive.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Brûlée is very loyal to her mother, as she followed her orders to keep Luffy and his group away from Sanji. She is also loyal to her family, as she went with Katakuri's plans to ambush the Straw Hats on their ship. She detests traitors, yelling angrily at <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> when she discovered him with the Sanji Retrieval Team,<sup id="cite_ref-c854_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c854-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> as well as questioning Chiffon in her participation in her husband's plot to assassinate their mother.<sup id="cite_ref-c858_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c858-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> She also became enraged at Pekoms for using her to assist Luffy in escaping.
</p><p>Brûlée is noted by her own family to be very careless and clumsy as proven when she easily ended up getting herself captured by her enemies for them to exploit her Devil Fruit powers as shown with Chopper and Luffy.
</p><p>Due to her arrogance and carelessness, Brûlée is very cowardly if she is caught in a helpless situation that would endanger her life. When Brûlée was being used by the Straw Hats and Fire Tank Pirates, she became terrified if her mother considered her a traitor and that she would be killed. When Luffy found her while he was retreating from Katakuri, Brûlée became terrified as she was taken hostage to escape the Mirro-World while pleading to Katakuri to save her. On Nuts Island, after being spotted, Brûlée pleaded for Perospero and Amande, and a deranged Big Mom to save her.
</p><p>Brûlée is tricky and deceptive, using her Devil Fruit to separate Luffy from his group by disguising as him and deceiving the retrieval team, and managed to capture Carrot in the Mirro-World. Though she is not always perceptive, as she failed to notice the frog transformed into Carrot was not actually speaking and also did not piece together that the duplicate mink came from her own Devil Fruit ability.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Brûlée also seems very susceptible to tickle torture, as she easily gave Chopper and Carrot all the answers they needed when they tickled her.<sup id="cite_ref-c851_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c851-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite being usually cruel to enemies, Brûlée has a kind and caring side as she genuinely loved her family, as she was crying when the Whole Cake Chateau was falling over with her family on it.<sup id="cite_ref-c872_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c872-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Even as a child, she tried to comfort Katakuri, telling him not to blame himself for her brutal disfigurement by his bullies.<sup id="cite_ref-scar_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-scar-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> She also tearfully reported Katakuri's defeat at Luffy's hands to her family and crew in order to ensure that neither he nor Sanji manage to escape.<sup id="cite_ref-c898p7-9_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c898p7-9-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> However, she was more concerned about Katakuri being hurt by Luffy rather than his loss against the latter. Brûlée cares for her brother in high regards, that she knew that Katakuri lays on his back and kept quiet about it out of respect towards him.
</p><p>Like other people, Brûlée has a unique <a href="/wiki/Laughter_Style" title="Laughter Style">laughing style</a>: "Wiwwiwwiwwi"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ウィッウィッ</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_2-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Charlotte_Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As her eighth daughter, Brûlée is very loyal to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">her mother</a>. Because of her loyalty, Brûlée followed her mother's orders in keeping Luffy from meeting Sanji.<sup id="cite_ref-c835p11_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c835p11-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Big Mom sent Brûlée's half-brother, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Cracker" title="Charlotte Cracker">Cracker</a>, to assist her against both <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> because Luffy was able to defeat <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Doflamingo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c836p7_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c836p7-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> When the Sanji Retrieval arrived at Big Mom's chamber, Brûlée attempted to shout for her mother's aid only to be gagged immediately.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Brûlée is also aware of her mother's complete ruthlessness towards her own children should they defy her<sup id="cite_ref-c858_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c858-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> as Brûlée was terrified that she would be murdered by Big Mom if she were considered an associate of the Fire Tank Pirates in their plot to assassinate her.<sup id="cite_ref-c859_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c859-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c864_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite her fear of her mother, Brûlée cried out for her when she was falling with the collapsing chateau.<sup id="cite_ref-c872_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c872-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Siblings">Siblings</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Due to her caring nature towards her family, Brûlée appears to be on good terms with a majority of her siblings. As maternal half-siblings, Brûlée and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Cracker" title="Charlotte Cracker">Charlotte Cracker</a> both get along very well. Even though Brûlée was annoyed that her older half-brother was sent to help her, they did cooperate in fighting Luffy and Nami.<sup id="cite_ref-c836p7_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c836p7-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> During the many times that she was captured by the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, her half-siblings, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Perospero</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Amande" title="Charlotte Amande">Amande</a> rushed to her aid when she called for help.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Oven</a> became enraged upon seeing <a href="/wiki/Pekoms" title="Pekoms">Pekoms</a> holding his "beloved" little half-sister, Brûlée at gunpoint and immediately saved her.<sup id="cite_ref-c897_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c897-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> During the Vinsmoke Family's escape, Brûlée cried when her little half-sister, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Pudding</a> was captured by the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, Brûlée bears open hostility towards any traitors to the family, such as her younger half-sister, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Chiffon" title="Charlotte Chiffon">Chiffon</a>, due to her joining Bege to kill their own mother, Big Mom. However, despite this hostility Brûlée has at least acknowledged Chiffon’s reasons for betraying their family as valid, as shown where she was silenced when the latter brought up the abuse she suffered under their mother. Chiffon would then tell Brûlée that her only family were Lola, Bege, and <a href="/wiki/Capone_Pez" title="Capone Pez">Pez</a> due to the abuse she suffered at their mother's hand.<sup id="cite_ref-c858_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c858-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Charlotte_Katakuri">Charlotte Katakuri</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After Bege's attempt to assassinate Big Mom failed, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Katakuri" title="Charlotte Katakuri">Katakuri</a> saved her from being used any further by their enemies and grabbed her by her collar as he noted that the enemy had been using her a lot in their plans. Brûlée showed fear in his presence as she frantically explained that she was a hostage who had no choice, before she implored her brother to finish off their enemies.<sup id="cite_ref-c869_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c869-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> She holds Katakuri's strength in the highest regard, as shown when she proudly bragged about it to Luffy while the Straw Hat captain was struggling in his fight against the Sweet Commander. She refers Katakuri as the Charlotte Family's greatest creation.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> She also cares greatly about Katakuri as she fanatically cried when Luffy defeated him<sup id="cite_ref-c896_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c896-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> and when she tearfully reported his defeat to her family and crew.<sup id="cite_ref-c898p7-9_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c898p7-9-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>They were extremely close since childhood since Brûlée does not discriminate against Katakuri for his pelican eel-like mouth. Even after Katakuri's bullies took revenge by scarring her face, Brûlée did not blame Katakuri and told him he is fine just the way he is. Later, Katakuri got his revenge by attacking the bullies for scarring his sister. Brûlée also has a habit of spying on Katakuri from the Mirro-World, thus learning all of his secrets including the fact he had laid on his back, which she kept to herself out of respect for the latter. It could be said that she is the only member of her family to respect the true Katakuri rather than an idealized version of him.
</p><p>Brûlée calls Katakuri affectionately as "onii-chan"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">お兄ちゃん</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-onii-chan_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-onii-chan-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> compared to the more neutral "nii-san"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">兄さん</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> she uses with Cracker.<sup id="cite_ref-nii-san_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nii-san-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> She also called Katakuri the absolute best brother in the world, which proves the immense affection and respect Brûlée holds for him.<sup id="cite_ref-c898p7-9_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c898p7-9-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Allies">Allies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kingbaum">Kingbaum</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Kingbaum" title="Kingbaum">Kingbaum</a> was loyal to Brûlée and respects her authority. However, when Nami pulled out Big Mom's <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card" title="Vivre Card">Vivre Card</a>, Kingbaum and the <a href="/wiki/Homies" title="Homies">Homies</a> stopped attacking Nami because they sensed Big Mom's soul.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Worst_Generation">Worst Generation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">The Worst Generation? What is so worst about it?!</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Brûlée's disdain for the worst generation.<sup id="cite_ref-c837p8-9_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c837p8-9-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
Brûlée mocked the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a> when they came to <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>. Only four known members before Luffy came: <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Eustass Kid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scratchmen_Apoo" title="Scratchmen Apoo">Scratchmen Apoo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Urouge" title="Urouge">Urouge</a>.
</p><p>Though Brûlée mocked the Worst Generation, she did acknowledge Urouge's achievement in defeating <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Snack" title="Charlotte Snack">one of the then Four Sweet Commanders</a>. However, Brûlée was proud to mention Urouge's defeat at the hands of Cracker.<sup id="cite_ref-c837p8-9_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c837p8-9-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Brûlée's dislike of the Worst Generation increased when she found out that Bege was really feigning loyalty and recruited Luffy in his plot to kill her mother.<sup id="cite_ref-c858_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c858-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sanji_Retrieval_Team">Sanji Retrieval Team</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On her mother's orders, Brûlée served as an adversary to the Sanji Retrieval Team and an obstacle in their efforts to rescue <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c835p11_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c835p11-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to Luffy being a part of the Worst Generation, Brûlée mocked him and the others from the same generation.<sup id="cite_ref-c837p8-9_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c837p8-9-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Brûlée is very antagonistic towards Nami and <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a>, saying that she wants to slice them because of how pretty they are.<sup id="cite_ref-c832_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c832-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> After seeing <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Hito_Hito_no_Mi" title="Hito Hito no Mi">abilities</a>, Brûlée took an interest in him and promised to collect him for her mother.<sup id="cite_ref-c835p13_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c835p13-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> After she trapped Carrot and Chopper in the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a>, she battled Nami, who managed to outwit and defeat her.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> After catching Chopper and Carrot in the Mirro-World, she prepared to put Carrot in boiling soup, although this failed.<sup id="cite_ref-c847_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c847-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Chopper and Carrot soon forced Brûlée into guiding them through the Mirro-World and helping them find their friends.<sup id="cite_ref-c851_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c851-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> She was angered when Luffy later used her powers to make copies of himself and destroyed the wedding cake that her mother was looking forward to.<sup id="cite_ref-c863p3-4_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c863p3-4-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After being freed by her brother Katakuri, Brûlée did not hesitate to stand in the Straw Hats' way of escape, determined to settle the score with them for using her.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> After the Whole Cake Chateau collapsed and the Straw Hats escaped, she told her brother Katakuri to kill them for all the time they held her hostage and she made sure to hinder their escape.<sup id="cite_ref-onii-chan_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-onii-chan-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> She took great joy in helping her family attack the Straw Hats' ship while Big Mom was chasing them.<sup id="cite_ref-c874_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c874-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Unfortunately for Brûlée, she was yet again taken prisoner by Luffy, who used her to travel from island to island through the Mirro-World. After seeing Luffy defeat Katakuri, Brûlée was extremely furious.<sup id="cite_ref-c896_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c896-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> On Cacao Island, she reported Katakuri's defeat at Luffy's hands to her family and crew in order to ensure that he and Sanji cannot escape.<sup id="cite_ref-c898p7-9_22-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c898p7-9-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> While complaining to her brother, she was upset that the Straw Hats managed to escape <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pound">Pound</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Brûlée made enemies with her former <a href="/wiki/Pound" title="Pound">step-father</a> and labeled him as an enemy to the <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">Charlotte Family</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c837p11_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c837p11-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jinbe">Jinbe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Brûlée was very enraged to see Jinbe with the Sanji Retrieval Team, saying that his actions meant betrayal to Big Mom. After Brûlée told Jinbe the true purpose of the punishment roulette wheel, she bragged that his actions would result in punishment by death, but her warning was ignored.<sup id="cite_ref-c854_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c854-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> She was later angered when he twice listed her as a member of the group to overthrow Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-c857_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c857-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pekoms">Pekoms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Pekoms captured Brûlée to use her to assist Luffy in escaping the Big Mom Pirates. Brûlée was infuriated at Pekoms' betrayal and bragged that he will be executed as a traitor.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As an officer of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>, Brûlée holds a high position in the crew and has authority over lower-ranking members.<sup id="cite_ref-c930_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c930-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Brûlée is a fairly powerful fighter, as Big Mom had enough confidence in her to prevent the Sanji Retrieval Team from escaping the Seducing Woods. She is also capable of coordinating with several homies in the forest to fight against them.
</p><p>However, her family notes that Brûlée is actually very clumsy and not as strong as she perceives herself. True enough, Chopper and Carrot were able to defeat her by using her powers against her and was even captured by an exhausted Luffy when he needed to escape from his fight with Katakuri. She was also easily captured by Pekoms and held hostage.
</p><p>Brûlée possesses a strong will, being able to withstand a burst of Big Mom's Haoshoku Haki and remain conscious from her loud scream.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Brûlée is rather strong, as she was easily able to lift and hold <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> by the neck with one hand. She also uses her long and sharp fingernails to slice people.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_2-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Brûlée also has fast reflexes. She was able to dodge <a href="/wiki/Pound" title="Pound">Pound</a>'s punch easily<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> and defend against Carrot, an extremely fast mink in her own right.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> She has considerable endurance, as she was able to withstand being scalded by a giant pot of soup as well as being electrocuted by Carrot's Electro and Nami's Thundercloud Rod, then regain consciousness shortly afterwards.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tactical_Skills">Tactical Skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>She is skilled in tactics such as ambush, traps, and trickery as seen when she easily separated Luffy from the Sanji Retrieval Team, sneaked up on Nami by disguising herself as Luffy, and easily trapped Carrot, a capable mink fighter, with only minimal effort.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Mira_Mira_no_Mi" title="Mira Mira no Mi">Mira Mira no Mi</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Mira_Mira_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20170709205701" class="image"><img alt="Mira Mira no Mi Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="315" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mira Mira no Mi Infobox.png" data-image-key="Mira_Mira_no_Mi_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Mira_Mira_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170709205701" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Mira_Mira_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20170709205701" class="image"><img alt="Mira Mira no Mi Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Mira_Mira_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170709205701" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="315" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mira Mira no Mi Infobox.png" data-image-key="Mira_Mira_no_Mi_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c3/Mira_Mira_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170709205701" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mira_Mira_no_Mi_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brûlée creates a mirror.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Brûlée ate the Mira Mira no Mi, a <a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allows her to create and manipulate mirrors.<sup id="cite_ref-intro_2-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> She can use her mirrors to reflect attacks back at her opponents, turn any mirror into a portal to the "<a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a>",<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> and transform herself and other living things into mirror images of different people.
</p><p>By creating a mirror shield, she can provide herself with an absolute defense that not only shields her, but also reflects an opponent's attacks back at them, turning their own strength against them.
</p><p>She can transform herself into a mirror image of a chosen target; while transformed into someone's reflection, she will do and say exactly whatever her target does and says, like a perfect reflection. The reverse is also true, allowing her to force the target to reflect her own words and actions.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> She can even reflect other people's Devil Fruit powers.<sup id="cite_ref-c831_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c831-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> She can also transform herself into a partial reflection, such as reflecting a person's body, but with her own face. This gives her access to that person's abilities and powers, but does not link the two to mimic each other's actions. 
</p><p>She has the ability to transform other living things, such as animals, into reflections as well, though these reflections are not linked to mimic the original or vice versa. This allows her to create chaos and confusion among her enemies.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/02/Mirro-World_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20170730020411" class="image"><img alt="Mirro-World Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mirro-World Infobox.png" data-image-key="Mirro-World_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/02/Mirro-World_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170730020411" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/02/Mirro-World_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20170730020411" class="image"><img alt="Mirro-World Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/02/Mirro-World_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170730020411" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mirro-World Infobox.png" data-image-key="Mirro-World_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/02/Mirro-World_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170730020411" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mirro-World_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Mirro-World.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>She can turn any mirror she touches into a doorway that connects the real world and her personal pocket dimension, the Mirro-World, a long tunnel filled with countless mirrors, each one connected to a counterpart mirror in the real world. Brûlée is referred to as "The Only Key to the Mirro-World"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>鏡世界</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>ミロワールド</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby>の唯一の鍵</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Miro Wārudo no Yuiitsu no Kagi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>;<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> without her, the mirrors in the Mirro-World are just mirrors, though they can be used as windows to view what is on the other side of their respective real world counterparts. She can use the Mirro-World to support her allies by allowing them to travel through the Mirro-World so that they can emerge from a mirror at an advantageous location.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c874_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c874-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c900_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c900-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> She can also use the Mirro-World to trap her enemies, as no one can enter or leave the Mirro-World without her.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>When she chased Chopper and Carrot inside the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a>, Brûlée wielded a scythe.<sup id="cite_ref-c842p6_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c842p6-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Medical_Expertise">Medical Expertise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Brûlée seems to have some medical knowledge as she tended to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Katakuri" title="Charlotte Katakuri">Katakuri</a>'s wounds after his defeat at the hands of Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-c902_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Brûlée and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Broy%C3%A9" title="Charlotte Broyé">Charlotte Broyé</a> were born as the eighth and ninth daughters of <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Charlotte Linlin</a>. When she was 5 years old,<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> some bullies whom her older brother, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Katakuri" title="Charlotte Katakuri">Katakuri</a>, beat up cut her face as revenge, giving her a massive scar that she would have the rest of her life. This caused Katakuri to get his revenge on them in return and he covered his mouth to protect <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">his family</a> ever since.<sup id="cite_ref-scar_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-scar-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Arc">Whole Cake Island Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Luffy_Meets_His_Reflection.png/revision/latest?cb=20170604020848" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Meets His Reflection" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luffy Meets His Reflection.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Meets_His_Reflection.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Luffy_Meets_His_Reflection.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170604020848" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Luffy_Meets_His_Reflection.png/revision/latest?cb=20170604020848" class="image"><img alt="Luffy Meets His Reflection" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Luffy_Meets_His_Reflection.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170604020848" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luffy Meets His Reflection.png" data-image-key="Luffy_Meets_His_Reflection.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d7/Luffy_Meets_His_Reflection.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170604020848" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luffy_Meets_His_Reflection.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brûlée poses as Luffy's reflection.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a> ventured into the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island#Seducing_Woods" title="Whole Cake Island">Seducing Woods</a> in search of <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>, Brûlée disguised herself as a mirrored version of Luffy and engaged in battle with the real Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-c831_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c831-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> When Nami, Chopper, and Carrot turned around and tried to escape, Brûlée went with them while Luffy was forced to run in the opposite direction. The <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates#Sub-Groups" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Sanji Retrieval Team</a> kept circling back to where they were before, before Brûlée revealed herself and grabbed Nami.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png/revision/latest?cb=20171117162455" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée Traps Carrot" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="274" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brûlée Traps Carrot.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171117162455" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png/revision/latest?cb=20171117162455" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée Traps Carrot" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171117162455" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="274" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brûlée Traps Carrot.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171117162455" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brûlée captures Carrot inside a mirror.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Nami quickly retrieved her <a href="/wiki/Art_of_Weather/Sorcery_Clima-Tact" title="Art of Weather/Sorcery Clima-Tact">Clima-Tact</a> and escaped Brûlée's grasp. Carrot then attempted to attack Brûlée, only for the latter to use the power of the <a href="/wiki/Mira_Mira_no_Mi" title="Mira Mira no Mi">Mira Mira no Mi</a> to reflect Carrot's attack back at her. When Carrot tried to attack again, Brûlée trapped her in the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a>, explained to Nami and Chopper that <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a> was well aware of their movements and had given orders to prevent them from meeting up with Sanji, and ordered the <a href="/wiki/Homies" title="Homies">living trees</a> in the Seducing Woods to subdue the two Straw Hats. When Chopper ate a <a href="/wiki/Rumble_Ball" title="Rumble Ball">Rumble Ball</a> and transformed, Brûlée was fascinated with his ability, and promised to collect him for her mother. While Chopper fended off the living trees, Nami ran away to find reinforcements.<sup id="cite_ref-c835_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c835-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> In the meantime, Brûlée had also used her ability to transform multiple animals into fake versions of Nami, Chopper, Carrot, Sanji, and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Charlotte Pudding</a>, keeping Luffy distracted with a chase through the woods.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Alongside the homies, Brûlée successfully managed to capture Chopper inside her Mirro-World. While riding <a href="/wiki/Kingbaum" title="Kingbaum">Kingbaum</a>, she arrived at the scene where her brother, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Cracker" title="Charlotte Cracker">Charlotte Cracker</a>, was confronting Luffy and Nami. She then reverted the animals that she had transformed into people back to normal and threw her mirror (that Chopper and Carrot were trapped behind) to the ground and shattered it into pieces. When Nami and <a href="/wiki/Pound" title="Pound">Pound</a> were fleeing the scene, Brûlée and the homies pursued them. However, when Nami took out a <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card" title="Vivre Card">Vivre Card</a>, the homies refused to attack her because they could feel Big Mom's soul from the Vivre Card.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Nami_Electrocutes_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest?cb=20170724131011" class="image"><img alt="Nami Electrocutes Brûlée" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="137" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nami Electrocutes Brûlée.png" data-image-key="Nami_Electrocutes_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Nami_Electrocutes_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170724131011" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Nami_Electrocutes_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest?cb=20170724131011" class="image"><img alt="Nami Electrocutes Brûlée" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Nami_Electrocutes_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170724131011" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="137" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nami Electrocutes Brûlée.png" data-image-key="Nami_Electrocutes_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0f/Nami_Electrocutes_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170724131011" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nami_Electrocutes_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brûlée is struck by Nami's Thunderbolt Tempo.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While Cracker was fighting Luffy, Brûlée was riding Kingbaum and chasing after Nami. Brûlée revealed that the Straw Hats were not the first pirates from the <a href="/wiki/Worst_Generation" title="Worst Generation">Worst Generation</a> that attempted to take down Big Mom, as <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Kid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Scratchmen_Apoo" title="Scratchmen Apoo">Apoo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Bege</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Urouge" title="Urouge">Urouge</a> had tried as well. They all failed but only Urouge was able to defeat <a href="/wiki/Snack" class="mw-redirect" title="Snack">one of the Sweet Commanders</a> but he was later defeated by Cracker. Brûlée then created and tossed a mirror to the ground and emerged from it, trying to capture Nami inside it. <a href="/wiki/Pound" title="Pound">Pound</a> saved Nami by trying to throw a punch at Brûlée, who declared Pound as an enemy of the <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">Charlotte Family</a>. Nami's Thunderbolt Tempo then struck Brûlée, causing her to fall defeated into the mirror.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
