<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest?cb=20171119162951" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Defeats Brûlée" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot Defeats Brûlée.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171119162951" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest?cb=20171119162951" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Defeats Brûlée" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171119162951" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot Defeats Brûlée.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171119162951" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brûlée being defeated by Carrot.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Brûlée later pursued Chopper and Carrot with a scythe inside the Mirro-World.<sup id="cite_ref-c842p6_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c842p6-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Brûlée eventually caught them and, after reporting the capture to her brother <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Mont-d%27Or" title="Charlotte Mont-d&#39;Or">Mont-d'Or</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> took them to <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island#Brûlée&#39;s_House" title="Whole Cake Island">her house</a>, where she made preparations to put Carrot into boiling soup, much to the mink's immense terror.<sup id="cite_ref-c847_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c847-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> However, Brûlée had actually captured a frog that she had accidentally made into Carrot's body double, and as she ordered <a href="/wiki/Randolph" title="Randolph">Randolph</a> to cut the rope holding Carrot's double over the soup, the real Carrot knocked Randolph over by throwing a rock at him. Not knowing he was attacked, Brûlée shouted at Randolph, but <a href="/wiki/Diesel" title="Diesel">Diesel</a> alerted her to the real Carrot hanging on the rope with the fake Carrot. Carrot then kicked the pot of soup at Brûlée, dousing her in boiling soup and defeating her.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Afterwards, Chopper and Carrot took her prisoner as they raced through the Mirro-World to find their friends. They tried to revive Brûlée to get her to guide them to the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Chateau" title="Whole Cake Chateau">Whole Cake Chateau</a>, but she remained unconscious.<sup id="cite_ref-c850_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c850-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Eventually, Brûlée was revived by Carrot tickling her, and Carrot and Chopper wanted to know where they could reach the castle. Brûlée revealed that she had forgotten and that they could ask the mirrors, and swore revenge on the duo.<sup id="cite_ref-c851_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c851-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Chopper and Carrot went and brought <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a>, Nami, and <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> into the Mirro-World, and Brûlée was shocked to see Jinbe, saying that his presence with the Sanji Retrieval Team meant betrayal. She heard that he avoided the punishment roulette wheel by taking back his request to leave Big Mom's crew, and when Pedro stated that the roulette meant certain death, she laughed and stated that he was right, affirming that no one left Big Mom's crew alive. However, she was interrupted as the Sanji Retrieval Team resumed their journey through the Mirro-World.<sup id="cite_ref-c854_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c854-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Chopper's group later located <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> and found him inside Big Mom's bedroom, being held in her hands as she slept. Brûlée tried to alert her mother, but Chopper and his group quickly gagged her. After the group successfully rescued Brook, Brûlée was shocked to see that Brook managed to acquire copies of the three <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">poneglyphs</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Later, Jinbe talked to Luffy through a mirror shard, and twice included Brûlée and Diesel in his headcount of their team, and the horrified duo quickly corrected him.<sup id="cite_ref-c857_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c857-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Diesel_Captured.png/revision/latest?cb=20180311224915" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée and Diesel Captured" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="126" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brûlée and Diesel Captured.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Diesel_Captured.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Diesel_Captured.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180311224915" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Diesel_Captured.png/revision/latest?cb=20180311224915" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée and Diesel Captured" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Diesel_Captured.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180311224915" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="126" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brûlée and Diesel Captured.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Diesel_Captured.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/94/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Diesel_Captured.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180311224915" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Diesel_Captured.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brûlée and Diesel tied up in the Fire Tank Pirates' base.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Brûlée and Diesel were then taken to the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Tank_Pirates" title="Fire Tank Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</a>' base, where they were left tied up. Due to Bege's sense of immaculacy, the two were cleaned up and given a set of clean clothes. Brûlée expressed outrage when she found out her sister <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Chiffon" title="Charlotte Chiffon">Chiffon</a> was taking part in a plan to assassinate Big Mom, but Chiffon reminded her of how poorly Big Mom had treated her and how she did not consider her mother family anymore.<sup id="cite_ref-c858_10-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c858-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As Bege went over his plan to kill Big Mom with Jinbe and the Sanji Retrieval Team, Brûlée objected when they planned to use her power to escape. Before the meeting adjourned, Brûlée wondered to herself with a nervous expression on how she could report to Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-c859_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c859-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> After the meeting, Luffy asked Bege to place a mirror inside the wedding cake. Brûlée expressed utter shock that Luffy planned to destroy the wedding cake, knowing how much Big Mom was looking forward to that. Planning to take advantage of Brûlée's power, Luffy later gathered a large number of animals so she could turn them into fake Luffys.<sup id="cite_ref-c863p3-4_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c863p3-4-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Brûlée and Diesel later slept alongside the Straw Hats inside <a href="/wiki/Shiro_Shiro_no_Mi" title="Shiro Shiro no Mi">Bege's body</a> as he set his assassination plan into motion.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> The team later went inside the Mirro-World, preparing to charge into the wedding venue. Once they heard the signal, they unleashed the Luffy duplicates into the venue and Brûlée cried in regret at not being able to defy Luffy's team.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> After the team and all of the clones entered the venue, Brûlée was left alone with <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Caesar%27s_Mirror_Breaks.png/revision/latest?cb=20180527091437" class="image"><img alt="Caesar&#39;s Mirror Breaks" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Caesar&#39;s Mirror Breaks.png" data-image-key="Caesar%27s_Mirror_Breaks.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Caesar%27s_Mirror_Breaks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180527091437" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Caesar%27s_Mirror_Breaks.png/revision/latest?cb=20180527091437" class="image"><img alt="Caesar&#39;s Mirror Breaks" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Caesar%27s_Mirror_Breaks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180527091437" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Caesar&#39;s Mirror Breaks.png" data-image-key="Caesar%27s_Mirror_Breaks.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Caesar%27s_Mirror_Breaks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180527091437" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Caesar%27s_Mirror_Breaks.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The planned mirror escape route is broken.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the ensuing conflict at the wedding venue, Caesar raced through the Mirro-World while carrying Brûlée, who continued pleading to stop being used to betray her mother.<sup id="cite_ref-c864_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c864-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> After they exited the Mirro-World and Caesar set up the escape mirror, Brûlée begged him not to allow her family to know that she was being used. Caesar then reminded her that her Devil Fruit powers were being utilized to cause the chaos at the venue.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> When Big Mom began screaming, Caesar flew in with Brûlée and the escape mirror, but Big Mom's scream shattered the mirror, causing them to be trapped in the wedding venue.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Bege then transformed into a fortress to save the alliance members. As Luffy's group and the <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmoke Family</a> ran into the fortress, Katakuri used <a href="/wiki/Mochi_Mochi_no_Mi" title="Mochi Mochi no Mi">his ability</a> and grabbed Brûlée from Caesar's back. Katakuri remarked to Brûlée on how her captors used her in their plan, but she replied that she was the victim and told him to make their enemies pay.<sup id="cite_ref-c869_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c869-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> When Caesar and Bege nearly escaped over the wall of the venue, Brûlée blocked their way by transforming into a double of Caesar, eager to pay the alliance back for using her. The Big Mom Pirates overwhelmed Luffy, Sanji, and the Vinsmoke Family. However, the <a href="/wiki/Tamatebako" title="Tamatebako">Tamatebako</a> dropped to the base of the Whole Cake Chateau and the bomb inside the chest exploded, causing the castle to topple over.<sup id="cite_ref-c871_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c871-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Brûlée then watched in terror as Big Mom's castle collapsed and her family fell with it.<sup id="cite_ref-c872_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c872-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> After <a href="/wiki/Streusen" title="Streusen">Streusen</a> saved the Big Mom Pirates by using <a href="/wiki/Kuku_Kuku_no_Mi" title="Kuku Kuku no Mi">his ability</a> to turn the castle to cake, Brûlée stood with some of her siblings as they organized groups to pursue the Straw Hats, the Fire Tank Pirates, and the Vinsmoke Family. Wanting revenge on the Straw Hats, she gladly joined Katakuri when he told her to follow him in his pursuit of Luffy. However, their plan was halted when Big Mom appeared in a craze. After <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Perospero</a> diverted Big Mom's attention to the Straw Hats, Brûlée listened to Pudding as she explained her plan to satiate Big Mom's craving.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Brûlée later joined with Perospero, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Daifuku</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Broy%C3%A9" title="Charlotte Broyé">Broyé</a>, and 10,000 <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land#Chess_Soldiers" title="Totto Land">Chess Soldiers</a> inside the Mirro-World. She reported to Mont-d'Or that her soldiers were ready to be deployed anywhere at a moment's notice.<sup id="cite_ref-c874_39-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c874-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> During a confrontation between Luffy and Katakuri on the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, Luffy grabbed Brûlée by the neck while she was standing inside the mirror leading to the Straw Hats' ship. She was then rendered unconscious as Luffy dragged Katakuri into the Mirro-World.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Her_Siblings_Attack_the_Sunny.png/revision/latest?cb=20190216225622" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée and Her Siblings Attack the Sunny" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brûlée and Her Siblings Attack the Sunny.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Her_Siblings_Attack_the_Sunny.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Her_Siblings_Attack_the_Sunny.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20190216225622" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Her_Siblings_Attack_the_Sunny.png/revision/latest?cb=20190216225622" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée and Her Siblings Attack the Sunny" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Her_Siblings_Attack_the_Sunny.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20190216225622" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brûlée and Her Siblings Attack the Sunny.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Her_Siblings_Attack_the_Sunny.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Her_Siblings_Attack_the_Sunny.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20190216225622" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_and_Her_Siblings_Attack_the_Sunny.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brûlée helping Mascarpone and Joscarpone attack the Thousand Sunny.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Brûlée later regained consciousness and Katakuri told her to set fire to the Thousand Sunny. <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Mascarpone" title="Charlotte Mascarpone">Mascarpone</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Joscarpone" title="Charlotte Joscarpone">Joscarpone</a> arrived and showed Brûlée another mirror leading to the Sunny. Brûlée laughed with glee as Mascarpone and Joscarpone shot flame arrows through the mirror. She then prepared to lead an invasion on the Sunny.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Brûlée and her siblings then received word from Perospero that Big Mom sunk the ship. Brûlée was pleased that she did not have to lead an invasion after all. However, Mascarpone and Joscarpone noticed by looking through a mirror to the Sunny that the ship did not appear to be underwater. They were then puzzled when all the mirrors to the Sunny began breaking one by one.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> As Luffy continued to struggle against Katakuri, Brûlée started bragging about Katakuri's legendary strength. Luffy tried to punch her, but Katakuri grabbed his fist. When Katakuri pondered on how he should maim Luffy with his trident, Brûlée told him to start with Luffy's neck. Having heard Luffy's conversation with his group and learning about their meeting place, Brûlée informed Perospero.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Brûlée then contacted Pudding and informed her about the Straw Hats' rendezvous point and that <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Oven" title="Charlotte Oven">Oven</a> would be at <a href="/wiki/Cacao_Island" title="Cacao Island">Cacao Island</a> to ambush them. She also encouraged Pudding to complete the wedding cake, saying that she was their last hope.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Brûlée was then found by Luffy, who was retreating from his fight with Katakuri. Luffy grabbed her and used her to escape the Mirro-World. They arrived at <a href="/wiki/Nuts_Island" title="Nuts Island">Nuts Island</a> and found Big Mom rampaging there. As she was held captive by Luffy, Brûlée cried out to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Amande" title="Charlotte Amande">Amande</a>, who was nearby. While carrying Brûlée, Luffy ran from Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> With Brûlée still captive, Luffy used her to escape from Big Mom and travel from island to island through the Mirro-World. While hiding inside a building, Brûlée was tied up as Luffy wondered how to defeat Katakuri.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_is_Held_Hostage.png/revision/latest?cb=20190210033806" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée is Held Hostage" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brûlée is Held Hostage.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_is_Held_Hostage.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_is_Held_Hostage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20190210033806" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_is_Held_Hostage.png/revision/latest?cb=20190210033806" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée is Held Hostage" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_is_Held_Hostage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20190210033806" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brûlée is Held Hostage.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_is_Held_Hostage.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_is_Held_Hostage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20190210033806" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_is_Held_Hostage.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brûlée being held hostage by Pekoms.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>She was later found and captured by <a href="/wiki/Pekoms" title="Pekoms">Pekoms</a>, who intended to honor Pedro's sacrifice by helping Luffy escape. As they approached Luffy, Brûlée was shocked and furious over Katakuri's defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-c896_32-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c896-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> While traveling to the mirror leading to Cacao Island, Pekoms explained his plan to help Luffy escape. Brûlée then explained to him that they have an army waiting for them on the other side. When exiting the Mirro-World, Pekoms used Brûlée as a shield as she cried for her family to save her. After Pekoms transformed into his <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong form</a>, Oven attacked him, causing him to release Brûlée.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702172548" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée Tends to Katakuri&#39;s Wounds" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="217" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brûlée Tends to Katakuri&#39;s Wounds.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172548" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png/revision/latest?cb=20230702172548" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée Tends to Katakuri&#39;s Wounds" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172548" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="217" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brûlée Tends to Katakuri&#39;s Wounds.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230702172548" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Tends_to_Katakuri%27s_Wounds.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Brûlée tends to Katakuri's wounds.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Luffy and Sanji were making their escape with <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a>'s assistance, Brûlée revealed to her family and crew that Luffy defeated Katakuri, shocking them all.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> Brûlée later brought her allies anti-Germa bullets, which they used to harm the Vinsmokes.<sup id="cite_ref-c900_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c900-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> She then went to attend Katakuri's wounds. When Katakuri regained consciousness, Brûlée told him that the Straw Hats had escaped from Totto Land.<sup id="cite_ref-c902_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c902-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="Germa_66.27s_Ahh..._An_Emotionless_Excursion"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Germa_66's_Ahh..._An_Emotionless_Excursion">Germa 66's Ahh... An Emotionless Excursion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Brûlée helped Oven transport the <a href="/wiki/Buku_Buku_no_Mi" title="Buku Buku no Mi">Prisoner Book</a> containing <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Niji" title="Vinsmoke Niji">Vinsmoke Niji</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Yonji" title="Vinsmoke Yonji">Yonji</a> to Whole Cake Island.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Shortly after, she reported to Cracker that <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Ichiji" title="Vinsmoke Ichiji">Ichiji</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Reiju" title="Vinsmoke Reiju">Reiju</a> were in Chocolat Town.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> Brûlée and Cracker went to the island to investigate and discovered that the invaders were not Germa 66 but instead were <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Van_Augur" title="Van Augur">Van Augur</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>. They failed to stop Pudding being abducted by the Titanic Captains, and the town and its people were <a href="/wiki/Hie_Hie_no_Mi" title="Hie Hie no Mi">frozen</a> by Kuzan. Brûlée was the only one to remain unfrozen, and she wept over being unable to save Pudding.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece_Film:_Red">One Piece Film: Red</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Uta" title="Uta">Uta</a> organized a concert on <a href="/wiki/Elegia" title="Elegia">Elegia</a> in order to realize her dream of performing for the whole world. Brûlée was present during the concert. She reluctantly teamed up with the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> to came up with a plan in order to defeat Uta and to battle <a href="/wiki/Tot_Musica" title="Tot Musica">Tot Musica</a> from within the <a href="/wiki/Uta_World" title="Uta World">Uta World</a>.
</p><p>Brulee used her Devil Fruit ability to help the Straw Hats escape Elegia Castle's crumbling basement after Nami's persuasion and later on, helps with rescuing the transformed concert audience to safety by entering them into her Mirro-World during the battle against Tot Musica.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Charlotte Brûlée (disguised as Luffy) vs. <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a></li>
<li>Brûlée vs. <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> and <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a></li>
<li>Brûlée and <a href="/wiki/Homies" title="Homies">Homies</a> vs. <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Tony Tony Chopper</a></li>
<li>Brûlée vs. Nami and <a href="/wiki/Pound" title="Pound">Pound</a></li>
<li>Brûlée, <a href="/wiki/Randolph" title="Randolph">Randolph</a>, <a href="/wiki/Diesel" title="Diesel">Diesel</a>, <a href="/wiki/Noble_Croc" title="Noble Croc">Noble Croc</a>, and Brûlée's twelve other henchmen vs. Tony Tony Chopper and Carrot</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Filler_Battles">Filler Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Brûlée and Randolph vs. Tony Tony Chopper and Carrot<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemy_Appearances">Enemy Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_4" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 4">One Piece: Pirate Warriors 4</a></i></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Support_Appearances">Support Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Bounty_Rush" title="One Piece Bounty Rush">One Piece Bounty Rush</a></i></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCharlotte_Br%25C3%25BBl%25C3%25A9e%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Her name is based on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cr%C3%A8me_br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:crème brûlée">crème brûlée</a>, a dessert made of custard topped with hard caramel, which follows the food themed names of the Charlotte Family and Big Mom Pirates.
<ul><li>Crème brûlée is also known as "burnt cream", possibly alluding to her defeat by being burned.</li></ul></li>
<li>Brûlée is the second character that was able to imitate the usage of the <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">Gomu Gomu no Mi</a> using its <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a>, with Brûlée using the <a href="/wiki/Mira_Mira_no_Mi" title="Mira Mira no Mi">Mira Mira no Mi</a>. The first was <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>, who used <a href="/wiki/Kage_Kage_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Kage Kage no Mi">Kage Kakumei</a> to manipulate <a href="/wiki/Oars" title="Oars">Oars</a>' shadow to perform the attacks.
<ul><li>In the anime, <a href="/wiki/Bentham" title="Bentham">Bentham</a> tried to fool <a href="/wiki/Magellan" title="Magellan">Magellan</a> by using Gomu Gomu no Okama Pistol, Okama Gatling, and okama Giant Scythe, though he only copied the naming pattern and not the attacks themselves.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>Brûlée shares a fairy tale theme with the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>:
<ul><li>Brûlée's general design and personality appear to be based on the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Queen_(Snow_White)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Queen (Snow White)">Evil Queen</a> character from the fairy tale "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Snow_White" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Snow White">Snow White</a>". This follows the general fairy tale theme of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Family" title="Charlotte Family">Charlotte Family</a>:
<ul><li>Both characters are shown to be envious of the beauty of a younger woman (in Brûlée's case, <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>).</li>
<li>In the original tale, the Evil Queen is known to disguise herself several times in order to trick the titular Snow White into killing herself. Brûlée follows a similar tactic, using her Devil Fruit ability to disguise herself in order to trick enemies.</li>
<li>The Evil Queen also speaks to a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Magic_Mirror_(Snow_White)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Magic Mirror (Snow White)">magic mirror</a>, which Brûlée's Devil Fruit power may be a reference to.
<ul><li>The mirrors inside her "<a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a>" also answer when being questioned, similar to the mirror from the fairy tale.</li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li>Brûlée's Devil Fruit may be a reference to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lewis_Carroll" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lewis Carroll">Lewis Carroll</a>'s novel, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Through_the_Looking-Glass,_and_What_Alice_Found_There" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Through the Looking-Glass, and What Alice Found There">Through the Looking-Glass, and What Alice Found There</a></i>, where a mirror acts as a portal to an alternate, mirrored universe.</li>
<li>Brûlée's attempt to eat <a href="/wiki/Carrot" title="Carrot">Carrot</a>, while inside a house made of cookies, resembles the witch from the famous fairy tale "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H%C3%A4nsel_and_Gretel" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Hänsel and Gretel">Hänsel and Gretel</a>".
<ul><li>Her defeat by being doused in the soup she was going to boil Carrot in mirrors the witch's demise, who was stuffed in the oven that the witch intended to force Hänsel into.</li>
<li>Brûlée's defeat by boiling water may also be an allusion to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wicked_Witch_of_the_West" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wicked Witch of the West">Wicked Witch of the West</a>, a witch character from the famous children's novel <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Wonderful_Wizard_of_Oz" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Wonderful Wizard of Oz">The Wonderful Wizard of Oz</a></i>.</li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li>Brûlée's appearance in a torn wedding dress may also be in reference to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Miss_Havisham" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Miss Havisham">Miss Havisham</a>, a twisted female character from the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>' novel <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Expectations" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Great Expectations">Great Expectations</a></i>.</li>
<li>Brûlée is the only antagonist in the series to correctly appraise <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a> as a reindeer upon seeing him, rather than calling him a tanuki and being corrected.</li>
<li>Brûlée was ranked by her younger siblings as their third-favorite older sister, behind <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Smoothie" title="Charlotte Smoothie">Smoothie</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Amande" title="Charlotte Amande">Amande</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Brûlée's favorite foods are crème brûlée and doughnuts.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
